simple-menu__body--plain py-4th" style="display: none;"><li><a data-login-modal-toggle-allow-untrusted-user="true" data-event-click-target="concerns#new" class="c-midnight-100 action-bar__button data-product-admin-id="79670" data-product-admin-model="Product" data-ue-widget="product-admin" class="x-product-admin-initialized is-hidden-default"><a data-login-modal-toggle-allow-untrusted-user="true" data-event-click-target="official_responses#new" class="c-midnight-100 action-bar__button text-lg ws-nw pl-half" ue=" login-modal-toggle" alt="Validated CJ Affiliate Reviewer" class="tag x-tooltip-initialized top" title="" ue="tooltip" aria-describedby="eet6yf-tooltip" data-yeti-box="eet6yf-tooltip" data-toggle="eet6yf-tooltip" data-resize="eet6yf-tooltip" data-tooltip="mz24ia-tooltip"><div class="d-f ai-c">Validated Reviewer<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" contain="paint" buffered-rendering="static" viewBox="0 0 16 12" class="c-teal-100 tiny ml-half icon-checkmark-thick nessy-only" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" role="presentation"><path d="M13.333 0L6.667 6.667l-4-4L0 5.333 6.667 12 16 2.667z"></path></svg></div></div><div class="tag x-tooltip-initialized top" data-container="body" title="" ue="tooltip" aria-describedby="ixb6vm-tooltip" data-yeti-box="ixb6vm-tooltip" data-toggle="ixb6vm-tooltip" data-resize="ixb6vm-tooltip" data-tooltip="3k98ez-tooltip">Review source: Organic</div></div></div><div class="paper__bd"><div class="d-f mb-1"><div class="f-1 d-f ai-c mb-half-small-only"><div class="stars large xlarge--medium-down stars-0"></div><div class="time-stamp pl-4th ws-nw"><span><span class="x-current-review-date" data-poison-date=""><meta content="2023-10-13" itemprop="datePublished"><time datetime="2023-10-13">Oct 13, 2023</time></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/cj-affiliate/reviews/cj-affiliate-review-8724153"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Missing Funds and Unresponsive Customer Support"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The ONLY thing I like about CJ.com is the common advantage of such affiliate platforms: it centralizes performance tracking and earnings from various campaigns into one account, reducing the need to interact with multiple companies or issue numerous invoices. However, the negatives have outweighed this sole benefit. After over a decade of affiliation, the severe issues I faced have led me to transition to direct affiliations with key companies. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I have been an affiliate with CJ.com for a decade now, and over the years I have always found their service to be lacking.
</p><p class="formatted-text">However, a recent incident has brought my concerns to a breaking point: at the end of August €7500, all being confirmed commissions set to be paid out, disappeared from my account with no trace or explanation.
</p><p class="formatted-text">Despite numerous emails and requests for explanations, I have yet to receive a satisfactory response.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">The support I have received has been lackluster at best. The affiliate support emails are disorganized and fail to address the core issue, leaving me in a loop of frustration. There seems to be a communication about some bank transfers, possibly three, initiated at the end of August, but none of them reached my bank account. My bank confirmed that no such transfers were received, and had there been any error in the details, the funds would have bounced back.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">I have repeatedly requested to speak to a payment department supervisor, to no avail. A few days ago, I was contacted by a team handling promotional campaigns for a publisher, and I seized the opportunity to report the issue once more and requested to be connected to a payment department supervisor. Yet again, my request was met with unhelpful responses that felt mocking rather than problem-solving.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">The lack of accountability and transparency from CJ.com has been appalling. Not only are my funds missing, but the inability to even discuss the issue with a responsible person is utterly disappointing. This incident has left me feeling helpless and exasperated. I share this experience as a cautionary tale to others who might consider joining CJ.com. The service, at least from my experience, has shown a lack of seriousness in addressing grave issues that affect the financial standings of their affiliates. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-8724153"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is CJ Affiliate solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The only advantage is the centralization of affiliations into a single account. But since the earned money disappears without explanations, it's not worth it anyway. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized x-login-modal-toggle-initialized" ue="toggle-class login-modal-toggle" data-resize="hvnuty-tooltip" data-tooltip="rjlq90-tooltip"><div class="d-f ai-c">Validated Reviewer<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" contain="paint" buffered-rendering="static" viewBox="0 0 16 data-toggle="6hqtzj-tooltip" data-resize="6hqtzj-tooltip" data-tooltip="bjoy6i-tooltip">Review source: Organic</div></div></div><div class="paper__bd"><div class="d-f mb-1"><div class="f-1 d-f ai-c mb-half-small-only"><div class="stars large xlarge--medium-down stars-1"></div><div class="time-stamp pl-4th ws-nw"><span><span class="x-current-review-date" data-poison-date=""><meta content="2023-03-23" itemprop="datePublished"><time datetime="2023-03-23">Mar 23, 2023</time></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/cj-affiliate/reviews/cj-affiliate-review-7860499"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Commission Junction stole our deposit and never give it back (6500$)"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">If you want to develop your business via affiliation, make your own affiliation program and develop it yourself by contacting directly the sites that are in your niche. Entrusting this task to Commission Junction and Advertising Purple is simply a huge waste of time and money. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">This whole sad story started with Advertising Purple contacting us with the promise of growing our online business through affiliate marketing with Commission Junction.  Advertising Purple claims to be the company with the largest number of affiliates in the U.S... something no one can verify and after this unfortunate experience is most likely false.  The cost of working with Advertising Purple + Commission Junction is very high between fixed and recurring fees. You have to pay between $5000 and $10,000 just to cover the future commissions of your future affiliates.  Here's how it really works:  Advertising Purple assigns you an account manager who only publishes your site on bogus coupon code and discount sites. The result is that even your customers who don't normally use coupon codes end up on these sites and ultimately make you lose money because without these sites, they would have bought at the price without a discount. In addition to not making you any money, you have to pay them a commission of course. All they do is bid on your brand name!  These coupon sites do not acquire new customers for you (or very few) but allow people who already know your brand to get discounts...so really NO interests at all.  Advertising Purple and Commission Junction promise you to be affiliated with quality sites (audience, traffic etc.) but in reality they are not. Their network literally stops at very poor quality sites with no interests. As for the account manager, let's call it "trainee" with 6 months experience, the word is more appropriate.  We have decided to close our account with both Advertising Purple and Commission Junction. We have been waiting for the return of our deposit at Commission Junction for almost a year now, which is about $6500! Commission Junction is literally stealing from its clients by confiscating the deposit that was given to them at the beginning of the contract. What a shame!  We have contacted our law firm to try to get this money back and our case is ongoing...  If you want to develop your business via affiliation, make your own affiliation program and develop it yourself by contacting directly the sites that are in your niche. Entrusting this task to Commission Junction and Advertising Purple is simply a huge waste of time and money. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-7860499 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is CJ Affiliate solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">They solved nothing hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-8079181 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is CJ Affiliate solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Impressed with CJ Affiliate's vast network of advertisers, flexible commission structures, and reliable payments. User-friendly platform with helpful support and resources for improving affiliate marketing skills. Highly recommended for anyone starting or expanding their affiliate network. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Positive experience with CJ Affiliate, but dislike high minimum payout threshold, the slow approval process for affiliate programs, and limited reporting and analytics tools. Still a valuable platform with a vast network of advertisers and flexible commission structures. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-7967573 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is CJ Affiliate solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">CJ Affiliate solves the problem of finding relevant products to promote by offering a vast network of advertisers. This benefit, combined with flexible commission structures and reliable payments, makes it easier for me to earn income through affiliate marketing. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted href="https://www.g2.com/products/cj-affiliate/reviews/cj-affiliate-review-5039520"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Intuitive Affiliate Platform"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">CJ offers an intuitive website that allows affiliate publishers to locate new and existing merchant partners quickly and identify essential details like commissions and contracts within a few taps. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The CJ website offers so many features that, at times, loading speeds are slow. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-5039520 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering CJ Affiliate:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">As a platform, CJ ticks all of the boxes for publishers and content creators looking for monetization solutions. The site itself is pretty intuitive — not as functional as Rakuten, but far and above a better UX than Impact. The team at CJ can be surly and brusque and often prioritize the needs of its merchants over interactions with its affiliates. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-5039520 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is CJ Affiliate solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">CJ solves the problem of identifying high-quality merchants relevant to our publishing space without the hassle of sifting through irrelevant products and services. Some affiliate platforms focus on quantity; however, CJ focuses on quality. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex class="paper__bd"><div class="d-f mb-1"><div class="f-1 d-f ai-c mb-half-small-only"><div class="stars large xlarge--medium-down stars-3"></div><div class="time-stamp pl-4th ws-nw"><span><span class="x-current-review-date" data-poison-date=""><meta content="2019-01-31" itemprop="datePublished"><time datetime="2019-01-31">Jan 31, 2019</time></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/cj-affiliate/reviews/cj-affiliate-review-1688567"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Isn't what it used to be"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">When CJ started out they had a very down to earth feel. Within the first month of beingvan affiliate with them they had sent me a wooden "money" train whistle with their logo on it. It was a way to say welcome and helped me feel welcomed to their company. That feeling is long gone. They have since been bought by a different company and you no longer feel any different then joining any other large affiliate program. They do offer a lot of affiliate programs in many categories and they have competetive commissions. I stopped using them after more then 15 years when they started charging me an inactivity fee, I was sending them traffic but my sales dropped off while I was restructuring my website. As mist people know the affiliate marketplace isn't what it used to be and CJ proves that point all so well. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Inactivity fees, no loyalty to websites that have been with the company for many years, they are much the same as all the other affiliate programs they don't stand out anymore. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-1688567 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is CJ Affiliate solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Earn money promoting other websites and brands through your own website. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c
